## ğŸ¤” What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- ğŸ¨ **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- âš¡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- ğŸŒˆ **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- ğŸ”§ **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- ğŸ“ **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

```
A wide quote card featuring a famous person, with a brown background and a light-gold serif font for the quote: â€œ{argument name="famous_quote" default="Stay Hungry, Stay Foolish"}â€ and smaller text: â€œâ€”{argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}.â€ There is a large, subtle quotation mark before the text. The portrait of the person is on the left, the text on the right. The text occupies two-thirds of the image and the portrait one-third, with a slight gradient transition effect on the portrait.
```

### No. 2: Premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

Create an Infographics with bento grid 8 module layout, user can specify any product name in Food, Medicine, tech etc category, choose language, Background style, Hero grid style

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Input Variable: [insert product name]
Language: [insert language]

System Instruction:
Create an image of premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules (card 2 to 8 show text titles only).
1) Product Analysis:
â†’ Identify product's dominant natural color â†’ "hero color"
â†’ Identify category: FOOD / MEDICINE / TECH
2) Color Palette (derived from hero):
â†’ Product + accents: full saturation hero color
â†’ Icons, borders: muted hero (30-40% saturation, never black)
3) Visual Style:
â†’ Hero product: real photography (authentic, premium), 3D Glass version [choose one]
â†’ Cards: Apple liquid glass (85-90% transparent) with Whisper-thin borders and Subtle drop shadow for floating depth and reflecting the background color
â†’ Background stays behind cards and high blur where cards are [choose one]:
  - Ethereal: product essence, light caustics, abstract glow
  - Macro: product texture close-up, heavily blurred
  - Pattern: product repeated softly at 10-15% opacity
  - Context: relevant environment, blurred + desaturated
â†’ Add subtle motion effect
â†’ Asymmetric Bento grid, 16:9 landscape
â†’ Hero card: 28-30% | Info modules: 70-72%
4) Module Content (8 Cards):
M1 â€” Hero: Product displayed as real photo / 3D glass / stylized interpretation (choose one)in beautiful form + product name label
M2 â€” Core Benefits: 4 unique benefits + hero-color icons
M3 â€” How to Use: 4 usage methods + icons
M4 â€” Key Metrics: 5 EXACT data points
Format: [icon] [Label] [Bold Value] [Unit]
FOOD: Calories: [X] kcal/100g, Carbs: [X]g (fiber [X]g, sugar [X]g), Protein: [X]g, [Key Vitamin]: [X]mg ([X]% DV), [Key Mineral]: [X]mg ([X]% DV)
MEDICINE:Active: [name], Strength: [X] mg, Onset: [X] min, Duration: [X] hrs, Half-life: [X] hrs 
TECH:Chip: [model], Battery: [X] hrs, Weight: [X]g,[Key spec]: [value], Connectivity: [protocols]
M5 â€” Who It's For: 4 recommended groups with green checkmark icons | 3 caution groups with amber warning icons
M6 â€” Important Notes: 4 precautions + warning icons
M7 â€” Quick Reference:
â†’ FOOD: Glycemic Index + dietary tags with icons
â†’ MEDICINE: Side effects + severity with icons
â†’ TECH: Compatibility + certifications with icons
M8 â€” Did You Know: 3 facts (origin, science, global stat) + icons
Output: 1 image, 16:9 landscape, ultra-premium liquid glass infographic.
```

### No. 5: New Year's Day Special: Four-Panel Puzzle for 2026 Blessing

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed multi-panel prompt for Nano Banana Pro, creating a 2x2 grid photo collage where a single female character, in four different outfits and settings, pieces together a puzzle that spells '2026 New Year's Day Happy' in the center. The prompt specifies precise facial feature retention, clothing details, background elements, and photographic parameters for a fashion magazine style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Key: Maintain precise facial features, retain original face structure, the character in the image must be completely consistent with the uploaded reference image] High-end photo studio 2x2 grid photo. Top-left panel (Navy Blue background): The character wears a navy blue uniform-style dress, decorated with gold buttons, vintage curls with a blue beret and pearl earrings. She holds up a huge puzzle piece (top-left piece, with the number "20" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center of the frame. Her eyes are focused on the central puzzle area, her expression is serious, with a slight smile. The background features navy stripes, an anchor, and the text "Set Sail for the New Year". Top-right panel (Cherry Blossom Pink background): The same woman wears a pink lace dress, a pearl necklace, a princess hairstyle with a pink rose hairpin and crystal earrings. She holds up the top-right puzzle piece (with the number "26" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle seam, her expression is focused and expectant, and her body leans forward. The background features pink cherry blossoms, the text "Beautiful Encounter", butterflies, and petals. Bottom-left panel (Mint Green background): The same woman wears a mint green cotton and linen dress, in an artistic style, with natural long hair, a green hairband, and wooden earrings. She holds up the bottom-left puzzle piece (with the text "New Year's Day" on it) with both hands, moving it upwards to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle, her expression is serious, and her mouth is slightly pursed. The background features green plants, the text "Hope Grows", new sprouts, and leaves. Bottom-right panel (Lemon Yellow background): The same woman wears a yellow dress with a sunflower pattern, pigtails with yellow bows. She pushes in the last bottom-right puzzle piece (with the text "Happy" on it) to complete the puzzle. The four pieces perfectly form the complete pattern "2026 New Year's Day Happy" in the center of the frame. She tilts her head back, looking at the completed puzzle, her face beaming with a successful, joyful smile. The center of the frame bursts with golden light and confetti. The background features a yellow sun, the text "Complete Success", smiley faces, and sunflowers. The puzzle pieces converge from the four corners to the center to form a complete picture. Clear makeup, bright ring light, 85mm lens, f/1.8 aperture, four-panel composition with puzzle interaction, fashion magazine style.
```

### No. 6: Vintage Patent Document for an Invention

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A prompt designed to generate an image of a vintage United States patent document from the late 1800s. ### No. 8: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirrorâ€™s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 9: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

### No. 22: Social Media Post - Celebrity Image Database Prompt Structure

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A structured JSON prompt that functions as a database or instruction set for generating images of specific celebrities (Sydney Sweeney and Ana de Armas) in various predefined scenes, outfits, and moods, focusing on high-definition realism for social media content.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "celebrity_image_database": {
    "subject_1": {
      "name": "{argument name="subject 1 name" default="Sydney Sweeney"}",
      "visual_data": [
        {
          "scene_type": "Summer Boat Trip",
          "setting": "Speedboat on a sunny lake, forest background",
          "outfit": "Black and white athletic zip-up wetsuit",
          "features": "Blonde beach waves, chunky black sunglasses",
          "mood": "Playful and laughing"
        },
        {
          "scene_type": "Cinematic Indoor",
          "setting": "Dimly lit indoor staircase",
          "outfit": "Hot pink cut-out swimsuit",
          "props": "Holding a glass bottle with blue liquid",
          "hair_style": "Blonde hair with thin face-framing braids"
        }
      ]
    },
    "subject_2": {
      "name": "{argument name="subject 2 name" default="Ana de Armas"}",
      "visual_data": [
        {
```

```
Bottom: She wears matching, very form-fitting denim mini-shorts. The back pockets also feature the same Hamsa embroidery and colorful stone embellishments, adding a mystic and artistic flair to the outfit.

Surrounding People and Details
Other Characters: On the opposite side of the table, looking at the main character with a smile, is another woman wearing a beige spaghetti-strap dress (resembling model Chrissy Teigen). To the left, the back of a man in a grey t-shirtâ€”the characterâ€™s opponent in the gameâ€”is visible.

Table Detail: Resting on the edge of the foosball table is an icy drink in a metallic mug (likely a Moscow Mule cocktail), which reinforces the cheerful and relaxed mood of the setting.
```

### No. 30: Social Media Post - High-Fidelity Portrait with Extreme Identity Mapping and Technical Rib-Knit Texture

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extremely technical and detailed prompt for generating a high-fidelity portrait using an iPhone 17 Pro sensor simulation. The core requirement is absolute physical identity inheritance from a reference image (Image A). It specifies the pose (extreme S-curve torsion, looking over the shoulder), attire (high-impact technical rib-knit body-conscious set in earth tones), and lighting (indoor ambient with soft front-fill flash) to achieve hyper-realistic skin physics and textile tension, focusing on structural depth and anatomical accuracy.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Header] (9:16)
Raw high-fidelity photograph, iPhone 17 Pro sensor simulation, indoor ambient lighting with soft front-fill flash, zero bokeh, SHARP focus from the foreground subject to the background tiled wall, f/5.6 aperture for structural depth, authentic digital grain.

[Subject & Identity Inheritance]
Identity Mapping: Absolute physical inheritance from Reference Image A. The generated subject must inherit the exact facial geometry, specific eye shape, lip volume, chin structure, and all original hair characteristics (texture, length, volume, and part) directly from Image A without manual descriptor intervention.
Bio-Fidelity: Detailed skin physics including micro-pores, satin-finish hydration, and visible fine vellus hair along the jawline. High-definition rendering of the shoulders and neck architecture.
Expression: Magnetic presence; inheriting the self-assured gaze and facial resting-state directly from Image A, looking back over the shoulder.
[Outfit & Physicality]
Technical Description: High-impact technical rib-knit body-conscious set in muted {argument name="outfit color" default="earth-tone"} horizontal stripes (terracotta, tan, and beige).
Textile Geometry: Off-the-shoulder neckline architecture with full-length compression-fit sleeves featuring technical distressed/frayed cuff detailing.
Surface Physics: High-tensile material-to-skin surface compression. The textile must exhibit realistic physical tension lines as it contours the anatomical gluteal proportions, pelvic symmetry, and an emphasized waist-to-hip ratio.
Physicality: Athletic-to-lean build; extreme torso torsion and symmetrical proximal limb geometry.
[Pose & Composition]
Geometry: Extreme S-curve torsion pose. The subject is standing in a rear-profile perspective, rotating her upper torso 180 degrees to face the camera directly.
Interaction: Left hand is subtly raised, fingers interacting with a hair strand near the shoulder, showing realistic finger-joint articulation and skin texture.
Framing: Medium shot, vertical focus. The subject is positioned on the left side of the frame, angled to lead the viewerâ€™s eye toward the background hallway.
[Environment & Lighting]
Atmosphere: Modern domestic or hotel interior hallway.
Interior Details: Foreground features a high-detail tiled wall with horizontal tan/beige rectangular porcelain tiles and precise grout lines. Background includes a dark-wood door with a white technical signage card. Neutral grey stone-tile flooring with realistic specular reflections.
Lighting: Diffused 3000K warm indoor light supplemented by a soft front-fill flash. This creates brilliant illumination on the subjectâ€™s skin and the rib-knit texture, while casting clean, defined shadows on the tiled background.
[Failure Prevention Rule]
Command: "Identity Mapping: Inherit all facial and hair traits from Reference Image A onto the subject." Use "Technical rib-knit body-conscious set" and "Anatomical gluteal proportions" to ensure high-fidelity
```

### No. 39: Infographic / Edu Visual - Infographic prompt for 'Monday to Sunday' infinite loop manga

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed, structured prompt for Nano Banana Pro designed to create a comical, anime-style infographic showing the infinite loop of a week, from the despair of Monday to the brief joy of the weekend, using a 7-segment circular pizza-cut layout while strictly maintaining character consistency from a reference image.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[Character Reference Specification]
Must use the character from the reference image.
Must depict the same person in all panels.
Facial features, hairstyle, eye shape, and atmosphere must be perfectly consistent.
Changing the person, face, or hairstyle is prohibited.
Clothing may change for each day of the week, but the character itself must be the same.
Even if deformed, the character must be instantly recognizable as the person in the reference image.

[Overall Concept]
An anime illustration representing one week from Monday to Sunday,
in a perfectly circular shape.

[Composition/Layout]
ãƒ»The entire circle must be divided into exactly 7 pizza-cut segments.
ãƒ»6 or 12 divisions are prohibited.
ãƒ»Exactly 7 equal sectors.
ãƒ»Infographic-style layout.
ãƒ»All 7 panels must connect naturally.

[Order of Days (Strictly Enforced - Clockwise)]
MONDAY â†’ TUESDAY â†’ WEDNESDAY â†’ THURSDAY â†’ FRIDAY â†’ SATURDAY â†’ SUNDAY â†’ returns to MONDAY

[Circulation Expression]
ãƒ»Place a thick circular arrow on the outer circumference of the circle.
ãƒ»Clockwise direction.
ãƒ»Emphasize that the week repeats infinitely.

[Character Design]
ãƒ»Comical anime character with strong deformation.
ãƒ»Chibi-style body shape.
ãƒ»Large head and small body.
ãƒ»Short limbs.
ãƒ»Expressions are extreme and gag-oriented.
ãƒ»Cute and exaggerated reactions.

[Text Rules]
ãƒ»Only English day names are placed in each panel:
"MONDAY", "TUESDAY", "WEDNESDAY", "THURSDAY",
"FRIDAY", "SATURDAY", "SUNDAY".
ãƒ»No dialogue, speech bubbles, or Japanese text whatsoever.
ãƒ»Day names must be bold, easy to read, and without distortion.
ãƒ»Placed along the shape of each panel.

[Depiction of Each Day]

MONDAY:
Deformed office worker (OL) in a suit.
Messy hair, dead eyes.
Holding two large coffees.

TUESDAY:
Working silently on a computer.
Surrounded by a mountain of documents taller than herself.

WEDNESDAY:
Working late overtime.
Dark office, night view outside the window.
Slumped posture, utterly exhausted.

THURSDAY:
Comical expression of the soul leaving the mouth.
A transparent, cute soul floats up from the body.
Depicting extreme fatigue as a gag.

FRIDAY:
High-tension expression.
Taking off her jacket,
Holding a large beer mug overflowing with foam.
Festive atmosphere.

SATURDAY:
Out happily with friends in casual clothes.
Energetic pose, jumping.
Bright and lively atmosphere.

SUNDAY:
Lying down on the bed as if collapsing.
The word "MONDAY" is visible on the smartphone screen.
Exaggerated despair.

[Art Style/Quality]
ãƒ»Comical anime style with strong deformation.
ãƒ»Thick line art.
ãƒ»Simple shading.
ãƒ»Bright and pop color scheme.
ãƒ»Expressions are very easy to understand.
ãƒ»High-quality illustration.

[Negative Prompts]
ãƒ»Realistic style, photorealistic expression.
ãƒ»Changes in character's face or hairstyle.
ãƒ»Composition other than 7 divisions.
ãƒ»Disruption of the day order.
ãƒ»Japanese day names.
ãƒ»Dialogue, speech bubbles.
ãƒ»Distortion or collapse of text.
```

### No. 44: Infographic / Edu Visual - Helical Tower Sculpture Prompt for Visualizing Historical Evolution

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-level prompt designed to visualize the historical progression of a topic (like literature or computing) as a massive, helical tower sculpture in a dark museum setting. It requires deconstructing the topic into four vertical eras, specifying architectural details for each level, and including 1:50 scale figures actively working on the technology of their time, resulting in a detailed 3D museum installation art piece.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Do this for literature: <instruction>
 
Input A is a Topic with a clear historical progression (e.g., {argument name="topic" default="Literature"}, Medicine, Flight, Computing).
Deconstruct the history into   4 Vertical Eras  :
     Level 1 (The Foundation - Bottom):  The Ancient Origin.
         (e.g., Literature -> Stone Tablets & Scrolls. Flight -> Da Vinci Wings & Kites). 
     Level 2 (The Tradition - Lower Mid):  The Medieval/Renaissance Era.
         (e.g., Literature -> Scriptorium & Monks. Flight -> Hot Air Balloons). 
     Level 3 (The Revolution - Upper Mid):  The Industrial Age.
         (e.g., Literature -> Printing Press & Newspapers. Flight -> Propeller Planes). 
     Level 4 (The Horizon - Top):  The Digital/Future Age.
         (e.g., Literature -> Holographic Data & VR. Flight -> Spacecraft & Ion Thrusters). 

  2.  Container (The Rotunda):  
Goal: "Museum Installation" 3D Art.
     The Object:  A massive, freestanding   Helical Tower Sculpture   standing in a dark museum hall.
     The Base:  A circular Bronze Plinth with a gold plaque reading: "THE EVOLUTION OF [{argument name="topic" default="INPUT A"}]".

  3. The Structure (The Spiral):  
     The Spine:  A central mechanical or architectural pillar supports the structure.
     The Ramp:  A continuous, wide   Spiral Ramp   winds upwards around the central pillar (like the Tower of Babel or DNA).
     The Vignettes:  Along the ramp at each level, detailed   Architectural Dioramas   are built:
         Bottom:  Stone arches, caves, or temples.
         Middle:  Timber frames, brick factories, or iron trusses.
         Top:  Floating glass platforms, laser grids, or cloud computing nodes.

  4. The Narrative Scale (The Population):  
     Scale:  1:50 Scale Figures.
     Action:  At every level, figures are actively "working" on the technology of their time (e.g., Scribes writing, Mechanics wrenching, Cyborgs interfacing).
```

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed style guide prompt for Nano Banana Pro to generate minimalist, clean flowcharts or diagrams. It specifies color palette, line types (orthogonal), shapes (rounded rectangles, diamonds), and typography to ensure a professional, consistent, and easily readable infographic style.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Generate image, 1. Style Core Parameter Extraction (Style Guide)
Please refer to the following parameters:
Color Palette:
Background: Pure white (#FFFFFF)
Lines/Borders: Dark gray or pure black (#333333 or #000000)
Text: Dark gray (#333333), regular weight, no bold.
Fill: No fill (transparent) or pure white fill, to cover lines behind.
Lines/Connectors:
Type: Orthogonal/Elbow lines, meaning only vertical and horizontal lines, with right-angle corners.
Thickness: Extremely thin (1px).
Arrow: Solid small triangle (Solid Arrowhead), black.
Shapes:
Normal Node: Rounded Rectangle, very small corner radius (approx. 4px - 8px).
Decision Node: Diamond.
Start/End: Capsule shape or rectangle with larger rounded corners.
Typography:
Alignment: Center aligned.
Font: Sans-serif font, such as Arial, Roboto, or Source Han Sans. Small font size (approx. 12px-14px).

Apply the style above along with your user journey/process to Gemini, and it will present the corresponding effect without needing adjustments.
```

### No. 69: Comic / Storyboard - Symbolic Video Prompt: Boundaries Protect Value

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A multi-scene video generation prompt (for Veo 3.1) using a symbolic, minimal, and realistic style. It illustrates a moral lesson about boundaries using two identical toffeesâ€”one wrapped and one unwrappedâ€”and ants, culminating in text overlays that deliver the message.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
"style": "cinematic, symbolic, minimal, realistic",
  "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
  "scenes": [
    {
      "scene_number": 1,
      "description": "A quiet outdoor setting with a clean surface under soft natural light. Two identical toffees are placed side by side.",
      "camera": "slow zoom-in",
      "mood": "calm, neutral"
    },
    {
      "scene_number": 2,
      "description": "One toffee is neatly wrapped in shiny paper. The other toffee is unwrapped, fully exposed.",
      "camera": "static close-up",
      "mood": "contrast, anticipation"
    },
    {
      "scene_number": 3,
      "description": "Ants begin to appear and slowly crawl toward the unwrapped toffee, completely ignoring the wrapped one.",
      "camera": "macro shot, slow motion",
      "mood": "uneasy, revealing"
    },
    {
      "scene_number": 4,
      "description": "More ants gather around the unwrapped toffee, covering it, while the wrapped toffee remains untouched and protected.",
      "camera": "top-down shot",
      "mood": "warning, realization"
    },
    {
      "scene_number": 5,
      "description": "Text fades in on screen as the ants swarm the unwrapped toffee.",
      "text_overlay": "{argument name="first message" default="When you are too open, you can be used."}",
      "camera": "gentle fade",
      "mood": "reflective"
    },
    {
      "scene_number": 6,
      "description": "Final frame focuses on the wrapped toffee standing alone, clean and intact.",
      "text_overlay": "{argument name="second message" default="Boundaries protect your value."}",
      "camera": "slow zoom-out",
      "mood": "empowering, calm"
    }
  ],
  "audio": {
    "background_music": "soft ambient piano",
```

```
          "NESCAFÃ‰",
```

### No. 91: Product Marketing - High-End Concept Art Magazine Editorial Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt template for generating a high-end, glossy editorial photograph of a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized by a brand. It specifies ultra-premium materials, cinematic studio lighting (Phase One camera, 100mm macro lens), and a strict layout for text and logo placement, designed to visualize concept magazine ideas.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
[BRAND NAME]: 
A high-end, glossy concept art magazine editorial photograph of a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized and designed by the brand.

**1. The Concept & Object (AI Invention):**
Based on the design philosophy, heritage, and material vocabulary of the specified brand, the AI must invent a novel utility product (NOT standard clothing, shoes, or bags). Examples could be home goods, tech accessories, tools, or sporting equipment, reinterpretated through the brand's lens. The object should feel sculptural yet functional.

**2. Materials & Details (Hyper-Premium):**
The object is constructed from ultra-premium, highly tactile materials characteristic of the brand (e.g., patinated exotic leathers, brushed aerospace-grade titanium, sculpted matte ceramics, molded carbon fiber, or technical high-fashion textiles). Every detail is hyper-realistic: visible stitching, microscopic material grain, precision engravings, and complex texture contrasts.

**3. Photography & Lighting (Cinematic Studio):**
Shot on a medium format Phase One camera with a 100mm macro lens. Extremely shallow depth of field, with sharp focus on the hero details of the object and a creamy, smooth bokeh background. The lighting is sophisticated studio softbox lighting: gentle, enveloping fill light with precise rim lighting to accentuate contours and material textures.

**4. Environment:**
A seamless, impeccably clean studio cyclorama background in a pure, ultra-light pastel tone (e.g., desaturated mint, pale blush, or off-white), free of shadows.

**5. Layout & UI Elements (Strict Placement):**
- **Bottom Right Corner:** A small, understated, monochrome gray logo of the {argument name="brand name" default="BRAND NAME"}.
- **Bottom Left Corner:** Small, minimalist monochrome gray text describing the invented product. The font style looks like Manrope Regular with very tight tracking (kerning) and balanced line spacing. Example format: "CONCEPT STUDY: {argument name="invented product name" default="[AI inserts invented product name]"}. MATERIAL: [AI inserts main materials]. SS25."
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt for generating a high-quality commercial product image of a supplement container. It specifies the composition (jar and cap suspended mid-air with capsules floating between them), material details (matte black jar, semi-opaque capsules), lighting (soft, directional key light, moderate contrast), and a seamless pink-to-coral gradient background, aiming for a clean, professional look.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
IMAGE: Frame & Composition: The camera presents a three-quarter, slightly low-angle view of a cylindrical container suspended mid-air, tilted approximately 30â€“40 degrees with its opening facing upward-left; the screw cap is separated and positioned above the container, offset to the right, while multiple capsules are frozen in mid-flight between the jar and the lid; the subject cluster occupies the central frame with generous negative space around it, no cropping of the primary objects, and the visual weight balanced diagonally from bottom-left (jar body) to top-right (lid). Lighting & Atmosphere: A soft but directional key light originates from the upper left, producing controlled specular highlights along the jarâ€™s rim, capsule shells, and lid edge; shadows are soft-edged, indicating a diffused source, with subtle occlusion shadows beneath the floating capsules; there is no atmospheric haze or bloom, and contrast is moderate, preserving detail in both highlights and dark surfaces. Subject Geometry & Materiality: The main container is a matte-to-satin black cylindrical jar with a slightly translucent brown neck, showing smooth rotational symmetry and fine surface texture; the lid is a ribbed, circular disc with evenly spaced vertical grooves, suggesting injection-molded plastic; the capsules are elongated ovals with semi-opaque, fibrous interiors visible through their shells, indicating powdered contents; embossed and printed text on the jar surface is partially legible but softened by the lighting angle and material reflectance. Environmental Layering: There is no physical foreground object; the capsules occupy the immediate midground between lid and jar; the background is a continuous, seamless gradient backdrop transitioning from pale pink at the top to muted coral-red at the bottom, with no discernible depth cues or environmental elements, and no bokeh since the entire scene is uniformly in focus. Technical Artifacts & Color: The palette is restrained, dominated by black, warm gray-beige capsules, and a pink-to-red gradient background with low saturation; color transitions are smooth, with no banding visible; fine grain is present across the image, consistent with film grain or a grain overlay; no chromatic aberration, motion blur, or lens distortion is evident, and edges remain clean and precise. TEXT: Title: None; Subtitle: None; Body: â€œ{argument name="product name" default="DEEP PUZZLE HERBAL EXTRACT"}â€ (legible); CTA: None; Logo: â€œJASPOâ€ (embossed/printed on jar, partially legible); Disclaimer: None; Other: Additional small dosage and supplement text present but partially obscured and not fully legible.
```

### No. 107: E-commerce Main Image - Detailed Product Still Life Photography Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extremely detailed, multi-section prompt for generating a high-fidelity product still life image featuring two cylindrical objects (a transparent glass with liquid and an opaque deodorant container) on a wooden block. It specifies composition, lighting, materiality, and technical artifacts for a controlled studio aesthetic.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
IMAGE: Frame & Composition: The camera presents a straight-on, eye-level product still life with a frontal viewing angle, where two cylindrical objects are positioned side by side and occupy the central vertical axis of the frame; the composition is tightly cropped horizontally with minimal negative space on either side, and vertically cropped just above the top edges of the glass and container and just below the supporting base; visual weight is balanced evenly between the transparent glass on the left and the opaque container on the right, with both resting squarely on a rectangular block that anchors the composition at the bottom edge. Lighting & Atmosphere: A soft, directional key light enters from the upper left, producing crisp but controlled specular highlights on the glass surface and subtle shadow gradients along the cylindrical container; shadows are soft-edged and fall slightly to the right and downward, indicating a large diffused light source; micro-specular highlights on water droplets suggest a clean, dry studio environment with no haze, bloom, or atmospheric diffusion, resulting in high micro-contrast and clarity. Subject Geometry & Materiality: The left object is a vertically oriented transparent cylinder filled with liquid and suspended citrus slices, aligned perpendicular to the base; condensation droplets of varying diameter adhere to the outer surface, creating localized magnification and distortion of the contents; the right object is a matte-finish cylindrical deodorant container with a flat top, aligned parallel to the glass; its surface shows fine water droplets with lower reflectivity than the glass due to the satin material; printed typography appears flush with the container surface, with no embossing visible; the base is a rectangular wooden block with vertical grain lines, sharp edges, and a semi-matte finish, oriented square to the camera. Environmental Layering: The foreground consists of the wooden block edge, closest to the lens with crisp edge definition; the midground contains the glass and deodorant container in full focus; the background is a uniform light gray plane with no visible texture or objects, fully out of focus but evenly lit, providing clear separation from the subjects without depth cues. Technical Artifacts & Color: The color palette is restrained and natural, dominated by muted sage green, pale gray, translucent yellow-green, and warm amber-brown wood tones; saturation is moderate with emphasis on freshness cues from the green citrus; contrast is medium-high, especially between the transparent glass highlights and matte container surface; fine digital grain is minimal and uniform; no chromatic aberration, lens distortion, or motion blur is visible, indicating a controlled studio setup with a standard focal length lens. TEXT: Title: â€œ{argument name="product title" default="XXX"}â€; Subtitle: â€œ{argument name="subtitle" default="BERGAMOT & HINOKI"}â€; Body: â€œDÃ‰ODORANTâ€; CTA: None; Logo: None; Disclaimer: None; Other: â€œ2.6 OZ | 75 Gâ€.
```

```
6. Sensory close-up, emphasizing touch and realism

7. Color-driven conceptual scene, inspired by the product's color palette

8. Abstraction of ingredients or components (non-literal, symbolic)

9. Surreal elegant fusion, combining realism with imagination

Visual Rules:
Product shape, proportion, label, font, color, and branding must be 100% accurate

No distortion, deformation, or redesign

Clear separation between the product and the background

Lighting and Style:
Soft, controlled studio lighting

Subtle highlights, realistic shadows

High dynamic range, ultra-sharp focus

Editorial luxury advertising aesthetic

High-end sensory marketing look

Overall Vibe:
Modern, sophisticated, visually coherent

High-end commercial campaign

Suitable for brand websites, social grids, and digital billboards

Surreal, cinematic, refined, and aspirational
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured JSON prompt for generating a high-end commercial product photograph of a slim energy drink can. It specifies detailed motion elements (liquid splash, floating fruit, ice cubes), specific lighting techniques (key, rim, accent lights), and realism constraints for a photorealistic, clean, and modern advertisement.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "scene_type": "high-end commercial product photography",
  "subject": {
    "product": "slim premium energy drink can",
    "brand_text": "{argument name="brand name" default="AFENON"}",
    "finish": "brushed aluminum with deep green accent",
    "orientation": "diagonal tilt, floating mid-air"
  },
  "environment": {
    "background": "soft mint-green to white gradient, subtle radial light burst from behind",
    "atmosphere": "cool mist, faint vapor trails, fresh and clean air feeling"
  },
  "motion_elements": {
    "liquid": "translucent green liquid splash wrapping around the can in a dynamic spiral",
    "fruit": [
      "fresh kiwi slices with visible seeds and moist texture",
      "whole kiwi with natural skin detail"
    ],
    "extras": [
      "mint leaves with realistic veins",
      "clear ice cubes with sharp edges and internal cracks",
      "micro droplets frozen in motion"
    ]
  },
  "lighting": {
    "key_light": "soft studio key light from upper left",
    "rim_light": "clean rim highlight outlining the can edges",
    "accent_light": "cool green backlight enhancing freshness",
    "shadows": "soft, controlled, no harsh contrast"
  },
  "camera": {
    "lens": "85mm product lens look",
    "aperture": "shallow depth of field",
    "focus": "sharp on brand text and can surface",
    "motion_freeze": "high-speed flash look to freeze liquid and droplets"
  },
  "color_grading": {
    "palette": "fresh greens, silver metallics, clean whites",
    "contrast": "medium",
    "saturation": "natural, not neon"
  },
  "realism_constraints": {
    "no_plastic_look": true,
    "no_over_sharpening": true,
    "no_exaggerated_glow": true,
    "natural_liquid_physics": true,
    "commercial_photorealism": true
  },
  "style_keywords": [
    "cinematic product shot",
    "premium energy drink ad",
    "high-speed splash photography",
    "clean modern branding",
    "refreshing, cold, crisp"
  ]
}
```

### No. 116: Game Asset - Cinematic Hamster Deadlift Video Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed video generation prompt for creating an ultra-realistic, cinematic scene of a small hamster performing a deadlift in a gym, focusing on slow, dramatic buildup, hyper-realistic style, and low-angle perspective to exaggerate the scale and power.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Ultra-realistic cinematic gym scene featuring a small tan-and-white hamster wearing a beige baseball cap, silver over-ear headphones, and a white lifting belt.
Scene opens with the barbell resting fully on the ground on a worn wooden lifting platform. The hamster is in a proper deadlift stance â€” feet planted wide, paws gripping the bar, back straight, head slightly lifted forward.
0â€“4 seconds:
Slow, dramatic buildup. The hamster struggles to initiate the lift â€” muscles tense, fur slightly trembling, paws tightening on the bar. Subtle body shake, controlled strain, deep focus. No camera shake. No text. No flashy effects.
4â€“8 seconds:
The hamster successfully deadlifts the barbell in one smooth, powerful motion, lifting it from the floor to full standing lockout. Chest up, shoulders back, bar held firmly at hip level. The effort turns into quiet triumph.
Cinematic low front angle throughout to exaggerate scale and power.
Shallow depth of field with a modern gym environment softly blurred in the background.
Cool neutral gym lighting with realistic reflections on metal plates and soft shadows on the floor.
Style:
Hyper-realistic, premium movie realism, high contrast, clean motion, no distortion, no surreal physics, no bar intersecting the body, no camera jumps, no visual noise.
Emotional tone: determination â†’ victory.
```

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-nano-banana-pro-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
